			| 6C24H: y := 0EBB3H

			| 5144H,6A3EH: y := 7F92H + x
			| 2237H: y := 0A1CBH
			| 6C18H..6C1AH: y := 7F96H + x
			| 6C15H: y := 0EBADH
			| 223DH,6A2FH,6A3DH: y := 7F9AH + x
			| 2227H,2228H: y := 7F9DH + x
			| 222AH: y := 0A1C8H
			| 6A35H,6C0DH: y := 7F9FH + x
			| 2229H: y := 0A1C9H
			| 6C07H: y := 0EBAAH
			| 6C05H: y := 0EBA9H
			| 222EH,6C06H: y := 7FA5H + x
			| 222BH: y := 0A1D2H
			| 2225H,6BFDH: y := 7FA9H + x
			| 2235H: y := 0A1DFH
			| 2234H: y := 0A1E0H
			| 2220H,6BF9H: y := 7FAFH + x
			| 4E38H,6A28H: y := 7FB0H + x
			| 221AH,6BF3H,6BF5H: y := 7FB2H + x
			| 6A17H,6A18H: y := 7FB4H + x
			| 2211H: y := 0A1C6H
			| 220FH: y := 0A1C7H
			| 6DFCH: y := 0EDB5H
			| 6BEAH: y := 0EBA4H
			| 221DH: y := 0A1D8H
			| 5F08H: y := 0DEC4H
			| 221EH: y := 0A1DEH
			| 2208H: y := 0A1CAH
			| 5EFEH: y := 0DEC3H
			| 69FFH: y := 0E9C8H
			| 4F0DH,69F2H: y := 7FDCH + x
			| 5FD2H,691FH,6920H,69EDH: y := 7FDDH + x
			| 53F3H: y := 0D3D2H
			| 69DFH: y := 0E9C4H
			| 69E0H: y := 0E9C6H
			| 69CCH: y := 0E9B3H
			| 69CEH: y := 0E9B6H
			| 4E07H: y := 0CDF2H
			| 69D4H: y := 0E9C0H
			| 5401H: y := 0D3F5H
			| 69CAH: y := 0E9C3H
			| 68FCH: y := 0E8FBH
			ELSE
				RETURN
			END;
			IF y < 256 THEN
				t[tW] := SHORT(CHR(y)); INC(tW)
			ELSE
				t[tW] := SHORT(CHR(y DIV 100H)); t[tW+1] := SHORT(CHR(y MOD 100H)); INC(tW, 2)
			END;
			INC(fR); DEC(fLen)
		END
	END Encode;

	PROCEDURE NewEncoder* (): Codecs.Encoder;
		VAR e: Encoder;
	BEGIN
		NEW(e); RETURN e
	END NewEncoder;

	(* Decoder *)

	PROCEDURE (d: Decoder) Decode (IN f: ARRAY OF SHORTCHAR; VAR fR, fLen: INTEGER; VAR t: ARRAY OF CHAR; VAR tW: INTEGER; OUT state: BOOLEAN);
		VAR x, y: INTEGER;
	BEGIN
		WHILE fLen > 0 DO
			x := ORD(f[fR]);
			CASE d.st OF 0:
				CASE x OF
				| 00H..7FH: t[tW] := CHR(00H + x); INC(tW)
				| 80H: t[tW] := 20ACX; INC(tW)
				| 81H..0FEH: d.b := 256 * x; INC(d.st)
				ELSE d.st := -1; RETURN END
			| 1:
				x := x + d.b;
				CASE x OF
				| 0E8FBH: y := 68FCH
				| 0E9C3H: y := 69CAH
				| 0D3F5H: y := 5401H
				| 0E9C0H: y := 69D4H
				| 0CDF2H: y := 4E07H
				| 0E9B6H: y := 69CEH
				| 0E9B3H: y := 69CCH
				| 0E9C6H: y := 69E0H
				| 0E9C4H: y := 69DFH
				| 0D3D2H: y := 53F3H
				| 0DFAFH,0E8FCH,0E8FDH,0E9CAH: y := -7FDDH + x
				| 0CEE9H,0E9CEH: y := -7FDCH + x
				| 0E9C8H: y := 69FFH
				| 0DEC3H: y := 5EFEH
				| 0A1CAH: y := 2208H
				| 0A1DEH: y := 221EH
				| 0DEC4H: y := 5F08H
				| 0A1D8H: y := 221DH

				| 0E8F3H: y := 68B5H
				| 0E9C7H: y := 698DH
				| 0E9B1H: y := 6978H
				| 0E8F9H,0E9A8H: y := -8037H + x
				| 0D3A1H: y := 5370H
				| 0E9C5H: y := 6995H
				| 0E9AFH: y := 6980H
				| 0E9B7H: y := 6989H
				| 0E9B4H,0E9B5H: y := -802DH + x
				| 0D4DBH: y := 54B1H
				| 0E9ADH: y := 6984H
				| 0CFC0H,0E9BBH: y := -8020H + x
				| 0E9B0H: y := 6998H
				| 0E9BCH: y := 69A7H
				| 0E9BEH: y := 69ABH
				| 0E9BFH: y := 69ADH
				| 0E9C1H: y := 69B1H
				| 0D3D6H: y := 53C8H
				| 0D4D5H: y := 54C9H
				| 0D3D1H: y := 53CBH
				| 0E8FEH: y := 68F9H
				| 0E9BDH: y := 69BBH
				| 0E9C2H: y := 69C1H
				ELSE d.st := -1; RETURN END;
				t[tW] := CHR(y); INC(tW);
				DEC(d.st)
			END;
			INC(fR); DEC(fLen)
		END;
		IF d.st = 0 THEN state := FALSE
		ELSIF d.st > 0 THEN state := TRUE
		ELSE HALT(100)
		END
	END Decode;

	PROCEDURE (d: Decoder) Reset;
	BEGIN d.st := 0
	END Reset;

	PROCEDURE NewDecoder* (): Codecs.Decoder;
		VAR d: Decoder;
	BEGIN
		NEW(d); d.Reset; RETURN d
	END NewDecoder;

END EncStdMap_cp936.
